:   "*Death is a natural part of life. Rejoice for those around you who transform into the Force.*"
:   ―Yoda[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_III-1)

 [![Death was a stage in life that saw the deceased become one with the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/OwenBeruDead-MOSW.png/revision/latest?cb=20131104064152) [![Death was a stage in life that saw the deceased become one with the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/OwenBeruDead-MOSW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131104064152)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/OwenBeruDead-MOSW.png/revision/latest?cb=20131104064152) 

Death was a stage in life that saw the deceased become one with the Force.

 

**Death** was the permanent cessation of all vital signs and functions of a living thing. When a life form died, their energy, their life passed from the [Living Force](/wiki/Living_Force "Living Force") to the [Cosmic Force](/wiki/Cosmic_Force "Cosmic Force") and became one with it, thus, the dead were part of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"), usually losing their individuality.[[2]](#cite_note-Voices-2)[[3]](#cite_note-Destiny-3) Death was a cause of dread and despair for most living beings, with some even vowing to defeat it and to keep people from dying, whereas others saw it as passing to the Force, a natural part of life.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4)[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_III-1) Some, like the [Nightsisters](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") of [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir"), were able to delay their spirit to be reversed into the Cosmic Force by shackling their spirit to the physical realm through [magick](/wiki/Magick "Magick"), while others, like the [Sith Lords](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord"), dreamed of [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality"). [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") was able to use the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") to [preserve](/wiki/Transference "Transference") his essence in a [clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") body. However, this technique couldn't grant him true deathlessness, as opposed to those beings who were able to maintain their consciousness after death by becoming [manifestations](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") of the Force.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-5)
